'JUG PA YIN LA, DE'I STENG DU CHU'I DKYIL 'KHOR RO, ,DE NAS NI
ME'O, ,DE NAS NI SA'O, ,DE'I STENG DU NI PADMA'O, ,DE'I STENG
GNAS PA'I SA BON NI MI SHIGS PA DANG,

YI GE'I MCHOG CES BRJOD DO, ,DBANG PO KUN LAS BYUNG BA NI, ,DAM
TSIG THOD PA ZHES BYAR BRJOD, ,MDZES PA PHRENG BA ZHES BSHAD DE,
,DE KHO NA NYID DBU RGYAN,

YIN; ;GTZUG GI NOR BU DBANG BSKUR TE, ,SANGS RGYAS ZHES BYA RJES
GNANG YIN, ,HE RU KA YI DBANG BSKUR BA'O, ,THOD PA LUS ZHES BYA
BA STE, ,RKED PA

PHRENG BA'I MING CAN YIN, ,DBU RGYAN BHA GA ZHES BYAR BRJOD,
,SANGS RGYAS KHUNGS [?] SA BRJOD DO, ,GTZUG GI NOR BU BDE BAR
BSHAD, ,RDO RJE PADMA'I DBANG BSKUR BYA'O, ,


@517A *, ,SLAR YANG BSHAD PAR BYA BA STE, ,THOD PA DBANG GNYIS
DAM TSIG STE, ,PHRENG BA SNGAGS KYI BDAG POR BRJOD, ,BCU DRUG
THIG GIS BTAB PA'O,,

STONG PA DBU RGYAN ZHES BYAR BSHAD, ,AA LA SOGS PA'I MA MO RNAMS,
,SANGS RGYAS ZHES BYA'I SGRA RU BRJOD, ,DE RNAMS DBUS KYI BDE BA
GANG, ,DE NI GTZUG GI NOR BUR

BRJOD, ,RIGS RNAMS KUN GYIS THAMS CAD DU, ,RTAG TU DBANG BSKUR DE
LTA BU, ,DPAL ZHES BYA BA DGA' BA STE, ,BDE BA SANGS RGYAS SU NI
BRJOD, ,PADMA PADMA NYID YIN

LA; ;NAGS NI SKYA RENGS ZHES BYAR GRAGS, ,RTZA BA BYANG CHUB SEMS
YIN NO, ,YANG NA, PADMA LTE BA'I 'KHOR LO STE, ,NAGS NI AA SOGS
MA ME YIN, ,RTZA BA THAR PA STER

BYED PA'I, ,BRDA YIS SANGS RGYAS PHYAG RGYA YIN, ,YANG NA, LTE BA
MTSO SKYES ZHES BYA BA STE, ,NAGS ZHES BYA BA NGAG YIN LA, ,RTZA
BA LUS KYI BLA DVAGS YIN, ,SANGS RGYAS

SEMS KYI BRDA YIN NO, ,GCIG PU NGES PA'I RNAL 'BYOR YIN, ,DBEN PA
RTOG PA SPANGS PA STE, ,SBAS PA GSAL BAR MA BYAS PA'O, ,NAGS NI
SNGAR BSHAD KHAMS RNAMS TE,,

LHAN CIG MCHOG TU 'JUG PAS NA, ,BSDUS PA ZHES NI BYA BAR BRJOD,
,LHA ZHES BYA BAR RANG MING BRJOD, ,GZA' DANG SKAR MA LA SOGS
LHA, ,AA GRA ZHES BYA'I SGRA BRJOD


@517B PA; ;DE NI RNAL 'BYOR SHES PA YIN, ,AA GRA GTZO BO ZHES
BRJOD CING, ,AA GRA DAM PA ZHES BYA LA, ,AA GRA DANG PO ZHES
BSHAD CING, ,AA GRA SPYI BOR GNAS PA'O, ,RANG GI MING DANG

LDAN PA YIS, ,SDIG PA DAG NI SEL BAR BYED, ,YANG NA SA NI AA SOGS
TE, ,DE RNAMS AA GRA HA ZHES BYA, ,MGOR GNAS 'OG TU BLTAS NAS NI,
,YI GE THA SNYAD TSAR DU 'BEBS,

THA SNYAD CES BYA BA NI, DBYANGS DANG, GSAL BYED RNAMS TE, ,DE
RNAMS KYIS 'TSO BAR GYUR PA'O, ,DBYANGS ZHES BYA BA LA, ,SVA NI,
RANG NYID KYIS SO, ,RA NI MDZES PA STE,

DES NA ME SVA RA'O, ,HA NI SKAL BZANG YI GE STE, ,RNAM PA'I MCHOG
KUN LDAN PA DANG, ,RGYAN RNAMS KUN GYIS KLUBS PA YIN, ,RDO RJE
SEMS SOGS LHA RNAMS SU, ,BDAG GI

LUS NI BSAM PAR BYA, ,BSAM GTAN SBYOR BA 'DI YIS NI, ,SDIG PA KUN
LAS GROL 'GYUR ZHING, ,BSOD NAMS KUN DANG LDAN PA RU, ,DNGOS PO
GSUM NI YANG DAG

GNAS; ;BRIS PAS BSOD NAMS GANG MTHONG BA, ,BSAM PAS KYANG NI DE
BZHIN MTHONG, ,SLOB MA BDAG NYID CHEN PO LA, ,'DI YIS DBANG NI
BSKUR BAR BYA, ,DBANG BSKUR

DAM PA BSGOM BYAR 'DOD, ,GANG DANG GANG GI LHA YI MCHOG ,DE DANG
DE NI SLOB DPON 'GRO, ,GANG DANG GANG LA LHAG MOS PA, ,DE DAG KUN
GYIS DBANG BSKUR BYA, ,DBANG NI RNAM


@518A *, ,PA BZHI DAG TU, ,YANG DANG YANG DU SO SOR BSHAD, ,GANG
ZHIG SNGAR NI BSHAD PA RNAMS, ,DE DAG KUN GYIS BRJOD PA YIN,
,RNAL MA'I SBYOR BA RTOGS BYA'I

PHYIR; ;BCOS MA YI NI SGOM PA DANG, ,BCOS MA YI NI BZLAS PA BYA,
,RNAL MA'I SBYOR BA RTOGS GYUR NA, ,BCOS MA'I SBYOR BA PHYI ROL
NAS, ,RNAL MA'I SBYOR BA RTOGS GYUR PAS,,

BCOS MA DAG NI MI BYA'O, ,DPER NA GZINGS LA 'JUS NAS NI, ,CHU YI
PHA ROL 'GRO BAR BYED, ,PHA ROL PHYIN NAS 'DOR BA LTAR, ,BCOS MA
DAG KYANG DE BZHIN NO, ,DKYIL 'KHOR

LA SOGS LAS GANG NI, ,BCOS MA'I SEMS KYIS GANG BYED PA, ,PHYI ROL
LAS RNAMS GSAL BYED PAS, ,DANG PO'I LAS CAN RNAMS LA BSNGAGS,
,DNGOS GRUB DE KUN 'DIR GNAS

PAS; ;RGYAL BA'I DNGOS NYID RIG LA MIN, ,GANG YANG SGRA SHES
BSTAN BCOS RNAMS, ,DRANG SRONG RNAMS KYIS BYAS PA LTAR, ,RANG GI
SEMS NI 'JUG BYED PA'I, ,SKYES BU'I BCOS

MA'I BYA BA RNAMS, ,RGYUD KYI RJES SU 'BRANG NAS NI, ,'BAD PAS
SDUG BSNGAL SLONG BAR BYED, ,DE PHYIR DKYIL 'KHOR LA SOGS PA,
,BYA BA'I CHO GA LA 'BAD PA, ,THAR PA DANG BRAL

PHYI ROL TE, ,SKYES BU NYON MONGS 'BA' ZHIG BYED, ,MI RTOG PAS NI
'TSANG MI RGYA, ,RTOG DANG BCAS PAS KYANG DE BZHIN, ,SHIN TU RNAM
DAG YONGS SHES NA, ,YID 'DOD RNAMS KYI DE


@518B NYID 'GYUR, ,RGYU DANG 'BRAS BU'I RANG BZHIN NI, ,DAM PA
NYID DU YOD MIN CING, ,RANG BZHIN GSAL BA NYID KYI PHYIR, ,STONG
PA NYID KYANG MA YIN NO, ,RANG BZHIN DBYE BA THAMS CAD KYI, ,RNAM
PA

DAG NI RNAM GNAS PA, ,RGYA MTSO LA NI RIN CHEN BZHIN, ,THOG MTHA'
MED PA'I TSUL CAN YIN, ,'JIG RTEN RTAG TU THA SNYAD SPYOD, ,'JIG
RTEN LAS 'DAS DE DANG 'GAL, ,YOD DANG MED

CES BYA BA NI, ,RANG BZHIN NYID DU SHES PA MIN, ,'DI YI TSUL GYIS
RAB RTOGS PA, ,RDZOGS DANG BRAL BAS GROL BA MIN, ,RNAL MA'I LAM
LA BRTEN NA NI, ,THAMS CAD BYAS KYANG

RNAM PAR GROL, ,SKYON DANG YON TAN 'PHEL BYED PA'I, ,'KHOR BA
DANG NI MYA NGAN 'DAS, ,BDE BA DANG NI SDUG BSNGAL DNGOS, ,LHAN
CIG SKYED PAR YANG DAG GNAS, ,MKHA' 'GRO KUN DANG

MNYAM SBYOR BA'I, ,RDO RJE MKHA' 'GRO BDE BA'I MCHOG, ,RDO RJE
SEMS DPA' DE BZHIN GSHEGS, ,BCOM LDAN RDO RJE CAN GYIS GSUNGS,
,RGYUD KYI RGYAL PO CHEN PO DPAL RDO RJE MKHA' 'GRO LAS,

RDO RJE SEMS DPA'I DBUGS DBYUNG BA DANG, RANG BZHIN NYID NGES PAR
BSTAN PA'I RIM PAR PHYE BA STE LNGA BCU PA'O,, ,,RGYUD KYI RGYAL
PO CHEN PO DPAL RDO RJE MKHA' 'GRO RDZOGS

SO,, ,,RGYA GAR GYI PAndI TA CHEN PO GA YA DHA RA DANG, BOD KYI
ZHU CHEN GYI LO TZ'A BA 'GOS LHAS BCOS KYIS BSGYUR CING ZHUS TE
DPE GNYIS LA GTUGS NAS GTAN LA PHAB PA,
